if (!is_file('composer.json')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: composer.json');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('composer.json')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): composer.json');
	} else if (sha1_file('composer.json') != 'f7061d18ffc0c793a59a22a3e1e3d534e020fb5f') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): composer.json');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('composer.json', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of composer.json');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('composer.json') !== 'f7061d18ffc0c793a59a22a3e1e3d534e020fb5f') {
		if (@sha1_file('composer.json') !== '7fa09ec8ee84041f8345454f623056c620782fb2') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: composer.json');
			$tmp = pathinfo('composer.json');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('composer.json')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('composer.json', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('composer.json') !== 'f7061d18ffc0c793a59a22a3e1e3d534e020fb5f') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): composer.json');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/objectTypes/oid/manifest.xml')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/viathinksoft/objectTypes/oid/manifest.xml');
	writefile_5();
	if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/objectTypes/oid/manifest.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/viathinksoft/objectTypes/oid/manifest.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/objectTypes/oid/manifest.xml') != 'ca37d1b9f30a8994ada89e046e214cd92f249c26') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/objectTypes/oid/manifest.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/viathinksoft/objectTypes/oid/manifest.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/viathinksoft/objectTypes/oid/manifest.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/objectTypes/oid/manifest.xml') !== 'ca37d1b9f30a8994ada89e046e214cd92f249c26') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/objectTypes/oid/manifest.xml') !== '12dc52038630d2d1a54de8f3696333ca8f49fd05') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/viathinksoft/objectTypes/oid/manifest.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/viathinksoft/objectTypes/oid/manifest.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/viathinksoft/objectTypes/oid/manifest.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/viathinksoft/objectTypes/oid/manifest.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_5();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/objectTypes/oid/manifest.xml') !== 'ca37d1b9f30a8994ada89e046e214cd92f249c26') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/objectTypes/oid/manifest.xml');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html');
	writefile_7();
	if (!is_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html');
	} else if (sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html') != 'a87ccaba449edb1a587bdbe65276bbc53cc1a359') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html') !== 'a87ccaba449edb1a587bdbe65276bbc53cc1a359') {
		if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html') !== 'a1323b5af64b533ae588d23b11de6d944f643f50') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html');
			$tmp = pathinfo('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_7();
		if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html') !== 'a87ccaba449edb1a587bdbe65276bbc53cc1a359') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): res/OIDplus/acknowledgements$dede.html');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
	writefile_8();
	if (!is_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
	} else if (sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html') != 'e10e340bd9b5487f43ec494a0cf4892cb7aaa7cc') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html') !== 'e10e340bd9b5487f43ec494a0cf4892cb7aaa7cc') {
		if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html') !== '178353ddd3e1734f99aac1729d4255518966af31') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
			$tmp = pathinfo('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_8();
		if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html') !== 'e10e340bd9b5487f43ec494a0cf4892cb7aaa7cc') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
		}
	}
}

} else {
	if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php') !== '959d3bfebdb3ef3e918fb300848287dfc66ad2d4') {
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php') !== 'f48d2f985f724ca800b9a81db63e12398084e25f') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_9();
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php') !== '959d3bfebdb3ef3e918fb300848287dfc66ad2d4') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/InstalledVersions.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('vendor/composer/installed.json')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: vendor/composer/installed.json');
	writefile_10();
	if (!is_file('vendor/composer/installed.json')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): vendor/composer/installed.json');
	} else if (sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') != 'e3792d3a640168e421db47f09ad2a79b781ba806') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/installed.json');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('vendor/composer/installed.json', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of vendor/composer/installed.json');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') !== 'e3792d3a640168e421db47f09ad2a79b781ba806') {
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') !== '7be6ac4c3f9af885dc493f088b29c4f613d86147') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: vendor/composer/installed.json');
			$tmp = pathinfo('vendor/composer/installed.json');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('vendor/composer/installed.json')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('vendor/composer/installed.json', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_10();
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') !== 'e3792d3a640168e421db47f09ad2a79b781ba806') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/installed.json');
		}
	}
}
